PUBLIC NOTICE
Mr. Gowri Shankar. K was born as a Male Child of Kuppusamy. C on 5th May 1994 residing at No. 54C, Velanthavalam
Road, Ottakkal Mandapam, Coimbatore-641 032. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living as a
Female (Reference Dr. S. Natarajan, MS. Professor In Surgery Chief Surgeon, Coimbatore Medical Collage Hospital,
Coimbatore-641 018). The thorough Clinical Examination under Dr. S. Natarajan, MS. Professor In Surgery & Chief Surgeon,
shows that I could be treated as a Female. Hence Gowri Shankar. K shall be known as KOUSHIKA. K
Chennai,
24th July 2017.

K. GOWRI SHANKAR.

K. Janarthanan a Male child born to Thiru S. Karunakaran on 9th April 1980 residing at No. 11/15, Nararajan Street.
Sekar Nagar, Jafferkhanpet, (West Side), Chennai-600 083, has been living as a Female after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. V. Jayaraman. By this, I, may be treated as a Female and shall hencefoeth be
known as K. MANU
Chennai,

K. JANARTHANAN

28th July 2017.
